3:13 *Fun fact.* Clear coca cola was actually invented by a guy named Georgy Zhukov in the 1940's as a request to the *Marshal of the Soviet Union.* The clear coke looked like a bottle of colourless caramel coloured cola with a white cap with a red star in the middle. This was supposed to resemble *Vodka* Back then, Coca Cola was banned from Russia, due to the world war.
